commit 7f52c723d2580572b6c53a04988f6f7d135bf36d
Author: karadoc <hidden>
Date:   2012-03-12 23:00:52 +1100

Added new function, CvPlayer::doesImprovementConnectBonus, which is meant to be a definitive indicator of whether or not a particular improvement will give the player access the bonus.
Cleaned up inconsistent and incorrect code throughout many parts of the code.
(Previously, there was some confusion in the code as to how such a check should be done. It turns out that there were _lots_ of bugs due to "isImprovementBonusTrade" being used on its own to decide if a bonus would be connected. The bugs affected a broad range of functions in the AI and in the UI; including the count of "unimproved bonuses" and "improvable bonuses", and worker build recommendations, and pillage evaluation, and so on.)

commit 2711e7fee3bc98f19cc19320427de63e5b6fbfd9
Author: karadoc <hidden>
Date:   2012-03-11 14:28:20 +1100

AI_civicValue now only counts the most valued potential corporation when speculating, rather than all potential corporations. Also, if when player does not have the prereqs for the civic being evaluated, then the prereqs are not checked for corporation speculation. (ie. the corps are valued regardless of whether the prereqs are met.)
Resource bonuses produced by corps are now valued in AI_civicValue.
Added new option to CvPlayerAI::AI_bonusValue, bAssumeEnabled. if bAssumeEnabled == false, and the team does not have the tech to enable or reveal the resource, the the resource is devalued.
Removed the default value for iChange in AI_bonusValue. There was some confusion as to whether the default was 1 or 0, and it was misused in many parts of the code, so I've removed the default and explicitly specified the parameter in all of the function calls.

Added a new function: CvUnitAI::AI_guardCoast.

Made several significant changes to the AI's civic evaluation.
 - When considering a civic which will disable corporations, the AI will now speculate about the potential of unfounded corporations and adjust the civic value accordingly.
 - Corrected an old, non-standard, yield multiplier. This will reduce the value of state property and of free speech.
 - Improved the accuracy of the capital city yield multiplier evaluation.

Standardized some code. (Added const to some functions, removed some magic numbers, moved some declarations, etc.)

commit 550a29006684f1cd1bc4171d28d689698bf3a4d0
Author: karadoc <hidden>
Date:   2012-03-02 15:24:00 +1100

MISSION_SKIP will now automatically unload units from transports if the mission comes with a not-trival MISSIONAI. (This is to prevent units from trying to guard cities while still in their transport.)
Disabled a bunch of BBAI code in continueMission which did some ad-hoc hackery for picking up strandard units. My new AI_handleStranded function doesn't require the old BBAI code, and the old code allowed the AI the cheat by allowing units to step onto a boat without needing movement points.

Moved the AI_load condition in AI_attackCityMove to be above the group condition, so that units don't leave their transports to group with their old stack!
In all of the naval Move functions: changed the city-under-threat condition to not include the case where there is no defence and not attack. (This is to allow boats to actually leave from undefended cities.)
CvUnitAI::AI_load, will now only split the group trying to load if the target transport is more than 1 turn away.

Adjusted pathCost to discourage units from ending their turn on tiles that they cannot fight on. (eg. boats in cities)
Added a new function, CvSelectionGroup::cargoSpaceAvailable. (currently unused)
Strengthed the condition for the AI automatically give a skip order to units on transports.

Rewrote the pathCost function used by the pathfinding. This fixes several pathfinding problems & bugs. Most notably, the new code allows the AI to choose a path with involves fighting through enemy units that are in the way; the new code does not take into account movement costs or defensive bonuses for tiles that have not been revealed (this makes the AI cheat less, but it also removes an exploit which allowed human players to determin the positions of islands, roads, etc.).
